 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="3"><B>Item&nbsp;2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="3">On February&nbsp;1, 2017, Baxter International Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) issued an earnings press release for the quarterly and annual periods ended
December&nbsp;31, 2016. The press release, including attachments, is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this report. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="3">The press release furnished as
Exhibit 99.1 contains financial measures that are not calculated in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;). The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures include adjusted operating
income, adjusted pre-tax income from continuing operations, adjusted income from continuing operations and adjusted diluted earnings per share from continuing operations, each excluding special items, and constant currency sales and free cash flow.
Special items are excluded because they are highly variable, difficult to predict or unusual and of a size that may substantially impact the Company&#146;s reported operations for a period. Net sales amounts are presented on a constant currency
basis. This measure provides information on the change in net sales assuming that foreign currency exchange rates have not changed between the prior and current periods. Free cash flow represents operating cash flow less capital expenditures. This
measure provides an indication of cash flow that may be available to fund investments in future growth initiatives. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures may provide a more complete understanding of the Company&#146;s
operations and can facilitate a fuller analysis of the Company&#146;s results of operations, particularly in evaluating performance from one period to another. Additionally, intangible asset amortization is excluded as a special item to facilitate
an evaluation of current and past operating performance and is similar to how management internally assesses performance. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="3">Management believes
that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings measures, when used in conjunction with the results presented in accordance with GAAP and the reconciliations to corresponding GAAP financial measures, may enhance an investor&#146;s
overall understanding of the Company&#146;s past financial performance and prospects for the future. Accordingly, management uses these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures internally in financial planning, to monitor business
unit performance, and in some cases for purposes of determining incentive compensation. This information should be considered in addition to, and not as substitutes for, information prepared in accordance with GAAP. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="3">The Company strongly encourages investors to review its consolidated financial statements and publicly filed reports in their entirety and cautions
investors that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used by the Company may differ from similar measures used by other companies, even when similar terms are used to identify such measures. </FONT></P>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Company Generated Full-Year Operating Cash Flow of $1.6 Billion and Free Cash Flow of $905 Million </B></FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">DEERFIELD, Ill., February&nbsp;1, 2017 &#151; Baxter International Inc. (NYSE:BAX) today reported results for the fourth quarter ended
December&nbsp;31, 2016, and provided its guidance for the first quarter and full-year 2017. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;Baxter&#146;s solid
operational performance in 2016 was fueled by strong sales and disciplined execution across the organization,&#148; said Jos&eacute; (Joe) E. Almeida, chairman and chief executive officer. &#147;We&#146;ll continue to build on this momentum in 2017
and beyond, driven by new product launches, effective portfolio management and further progress on our business transformation initiatives &#151; all in support of delivering sustainable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-quartile</FONT> results
for our shareholders, and advancing our mission to save and sustain lives.&#148; </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- more -
</FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U> BAXTER REPORTS 2016 FOURTH-QUARTER AND FULL-YEAR RESULTS&nbsp;&#151;&nbsp;Page&nbsp;
 2
 </U></B></FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Fourth-Quarter Financial Results </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Baxter reported income from continuing operations of $240&nbsp;million, or $0.44 per diluted share, on a GAAP (Generally Accepted Accounting Principles) basis for the fourth quarter. These results
included special items totaling $134&nbsp;million ($72&nbsp;million net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax),</FONT> primarily related to business optimization initiatives and intangible asset
amortization.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On an adjusted
basis, excluding special items, Baxter&#146;s fourth quarter income from continuing operations totaled $312&nbsp;million, or $0.57 per diluted share, exceeding the company&#146;s previously issued guidance of $0.49 to $0.52 per diluted share.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Baxter&#146;s worldwide sales totaled $2.6&nbsp;billion in the fourth quarter, an increase of 2&nbsp;percent on both a
reported and constant currency basis as compared to the prior-year period. Sales within the U.S. were $1.1&nbsp;billion, advancing 5&nbsp;percent, while international sales totaled $1.5&nbsp;billion, representing a 1&nbsp;percent decrease on a
reported basis, and an increase of 1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Adjusting for the impact of foreign exchange and generic competition for cyclophosphamide, Baxter&#146;s sales increased 7&nbsp;percent in the U.S. and rose
3&nbsp;percent globally in the fourth quarter. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">By business, Hospital Products sales of $1.6&nbsp;billion in the fourth quarter
increased 1&nbsp;percent on a reported basis, and 1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Adjusting for the impact of foreign exchange and cyclophosphamide, Hospital Products sales advanced 2&nbsp;percent from the prior-year period. Hospital
Products performance in the quarter benefited from strong sales of IV therapies, infusion pumps and related IV access administration sets in the U.S., along with </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- more -
</FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U> BAXTER REPORTS 2016 FOURTH-QUARTER AND FULL-YEAR RESULTS&nbsp;&#151;&nbsp;Page&nbsp;
 3
 </U></B></FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">favorable
demand for anesthesia and critical care products globally. This performance was partially offset by lower sales of IV solutions internationally, as the company implements actions to optimize its global product portfolio, as well as lower
manufacturing service revenues from Shire, under the company&#146;s manufacturing and supply agreement with Baxalta. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Baxter&#146;s Renal sales totaled $1&nbsp;billion in the fourth quarter, representing a 3&nbsp;percent increase on a reported basis, and a
5&nbsp;percent increase on a constant currency basis. U.S. sales grew 7&nbsp;percent to $222&nbsp;million, and international sales totaled $793&nbsp;million, representing growth of 2&nbsp;percent on a reported basis, and an increase of
4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Growth continued to be driven by robust sales of peritoneal dialysis products as well as increased demand for the company&#146;s acute renal care products. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">During the quarter, Baxter repurchased $247 million worth of common stock or approximately 5.4 million shares outstanding. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Summary of Full-Year 2016 Results </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For full-year 2016, Baxter reported income from continuing operations of approximately $5&nbsp;billion, or $9.01 per diluted share, on a GAAP basis. These results included a gain of $4.4&nbsp;billion (on
a pre and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">post-tax</FONT> basis), related to the company&#146;s disposition of its retained Baxalta shares. Partially offsetting these results were special items of $817&nbsp;million ($557&nbsp;million net <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax)</FONT> related to business optimization initiatives, intangible asset amortization, debt extinguishment costs, Baxalta-related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">spin-off</FONT> costs and asset impairments.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On an adjusted basis, excluding special items, Baxter&#146;s full-year income from continuing operations totaled
$1.1&nbsp;billion, or $1.96 per diluted share. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- more -
</FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U> BAXTER REPORTS 2016 FOURTH-QUARTER AND FULL-YEAR RESULTS&nbsp;&#151;&nbsp;Page&nbsp;
 4
 </U></B></FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Baxter&#146;s worldwide sales totaled $10.2&nbsp;billion in 2016, an increase of 2&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and 4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis as compared to the prior year. Sales
within the United States totaled $4.3&nbsp;billion, improving 6&nbsp;percent over the prior year. International sales totaled $5.9&nbsp;billion, representing a 1&nbsp;percent decrease on a reported basis, and an increase of 3&nbsp;percent on a
constant currency basis. Adjusting for the impact of foreign exchange and generic competition for cyclophosphamide, Baxter&#146;s sales increased 9&nbsp;percent in the U.S. and rose 5&nbsp;percent globally. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Full-year sales for Hospital Products totaled $6.3&nbsp;billion, reflecting growth of 2&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and
4&nbsp;percent at constant currency. Adjusting for the impact of foreign exchange and cyclophosphamide, sales increased 5&nbsp;percent. Baxter&#146;s Renal sales totaled $3.9&nbsp;billion, increasing 2 and 5&nbsp;percent on a reported and constant
currency basis, respectively. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In 2016, Baxter generated $1.6&nbsp;billion in operating cash flow, an increase of
$371&nbsp;million driven by improved operational performance and implementation of new programs focused on improving the company&#146;s working capital. In addition, through disciplined management of expenditures Baxter reduced capital spending by
$192&nbsp;million to $711&nbsp;million. As a result, the company generated an increase of $563&nbsp;million in free cash flow to $905&nbsp;million (operating cash flow less capital expenditures). </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#147;We are extremely pleased with the significant improvements Baxter has made in free cash flow generation. Our progress in 2016
represented an increase of more than 2.5 times as compared to 2015, and further supports our ability to reinvest in the business both organically and inorganically to drive accelerated growth,&#148; said Jay Saccaro, Baxter&#146;s chief financial
officer. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- more -
</FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U> BAXTER REPORTS 2016 FOURTH-QUARTER AND FULL-YEAR RESULTS&nbsp;&#151;&nbsp;Page&nbsp;
 5
 </U></B></FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Business
Highlights </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In 2016 Baxter continued delivering meaningful innovation for patients and expanded access to life-sustaining
therapies through a combination of more than 20 new product launches, line extensions and geographic expansions, including: NUMETA G13E, the only triple-chamber commercially prepared parenteral nutrition system approved for vulnerable neonatal
patients; HEMOPATCH, an advanced surgical patch; premix generic drugs such as VANCOMYCIN injection in 0.9% Sodium Chloride; new applications and features for the SIGMA SPECTRUM infusion system; and HDx therapy enabled by THERANOVA to provide high
performance hemodialysis treatments. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Additionally, the company saw continued momentum with its new Automated Peritoneal
Dialysis (APD) systems, AMIA in the U.S. and HOMECHOICE CLARIA outside the U.S., both featuring Baxter&#146;s SHARESOURCE Connectivity Platform, the first and only <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">two-way</FONT> remote patient management system for
home dialysis therapy. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In December, Baxter announced plans to expand its presence in the generic injectables space with the
proposed acquisition of Claris Injectables Limited (Claris). The acquisition of Claris, which is expected to close in the second half of 2017, will provide Baxter with a currently marketed portfolio of molecules in anesthesia and analgesics, renal,
anti-infectives and critical care in a variety of presentations including bags, vials and ampoules, along with a robust pipeline and high-quality manufacturing capabilities. This acquisition will provide Baxter with a platform to establish a
leadership position in generic injectables. </FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">- more -
</FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U> BAXTER REPORTS 2016 FOURTH-QUARTER AND FULL-YEAR RESULTS&nbsp;&#151;&nbsp;Page&nbsp;
 6
 </U></B></FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Over the course of the year, the company also took actions to significantly improve its balance sheet position and return value to shareholders through the disposition of the Baxalta retained stake, a
$1.6&nbsp;billion debt offering to retire existing higher coupon rate bonds and pay off outstanding commercial paper, a 13&nbsp;percent increase in its shareholder dividend and share repurchases of approximately $300&nbsp;million. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Financial Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Baxter is providing its outlook for the full-year and first quarter of 2017: </FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U>For full-year 2017</U>, Baxter expects sales to be comparable to the prior-year period on a reported basis and to increase approximately
2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. Adjusting for the impact of generic cyclophosphamide competition (an estimated one percent) and selected strategic product exits the company is undertaking (an estimated one percent), Baxter expects
underlying constant currency sales growth of approximately 4&nbsp;percent. The company expects earnings from continuing operations, before special items, of $2.10 to $2.18 per diluted share. This guidance does not include any impact from the

$1.67</FONT></FONT></TD></TR>

events or new information may result in different actual results. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A webcast of Baxter&#146;s fourth quarter investor
conference call can be accessed live from a link on the company&#146;s website at www.baxter.com beginning at 7:30 a.m. CST on February&nbsp;1, 2017. Please visit the Investors section at <U>www.baxter.com</U> for a supplemental presentation
regarding fourth quarter and full-year performance, as well as for information on future investor events and webcasts. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Baxter
provides a broad portfolio of essential renal and hospital products, including home, acute and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-center</FONT> dialysis; sterile IV solutions; infusion systems

 </U></B></FONT></P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">and
devices; parenteral nutrition; biosurgery products and anesthetics; and pharmacy automation, software and services. The company&#146;s global footprint and the critical nature of its products and services play a key role in expanding access to
healthcare in emerging and developed countries. Baxter&#146;s employees worldwide are building upon the company&#146;s rich heritage of medical breakthroughs to advance the next generation of healthcare innovations that enable patient care.

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The company&#146;s results in 2016 included a net charge of $409&nbsp;million ($290&nbsp;million, or $0.53 per diluted share, on an <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> basis) related to business optimization initiatives. This included a net charge of $285&nbsp;million related to restructuring activities, $65&nbsp;million of costs to implement business optimization
programs which primarily included external consulting and project employee costs, $33&nbsp;million of accelerated depreciation associated with facilities to be closed, and $26&nbsp;million of Gambro integration costs. The $285&nbsp;million of net
restructuring charges included net $180&nbsp;million of employee termination costs, $54&nbsp;million of costs related to the discontinuance of the VIVIA home hemodialysis development program, $47&nbsp;million of asset impairment charges related to
acquired <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-process</FONT> R&amp;D and facility closure costs, and net $4&nbsp;million of other exit costs. </FONT></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

STYLE="vertical-align:baseline; position:relative; bottom:.8ex"></SUP></FONT></B>The company&#146;s results in 2015 included a net charge of $200&nbsp;million ($141&nbsp;million, or $0.26 per diluted share, on an
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> basis) primarily related to business optimization charges. This included a net charge of $127&nbsp;million related to restructuring activities and $73&nbsp;million of Gambro integration costs. The
$127&nbsp;million of net restructuring charges included net $91&nbsp;million of employee termination costs, a $20&nbsp;million intangible asset impairment, and $16&nbsp;million of asset and other exit costs. </FONT></P>
